     5	@MainActor
     6	final class SettingsWindow {
     7	    private var window: NSWindow?
     8	    private let viewModel: SettingsViewModel
     9	
    10	    init(viewModel: SettingsViewModel) {
    11	        self.viewModel = viewModel
    12	    }
    13	
    14	    func show() {
    15	        if window == nil {
    16	            let window = NSWindow(
    17	                contentRect: NSRect(x: 0, y: 0, width: 500, height: 500),
    18	                styleMask: [.titled, .closable, .resizable],
    19	                backing: .buffered,
    20	                defer: false
    21	            )
    22	            window.title = "MaxMi Settings"
    23	            window.center()
    24	            window.contentViewController = NSHostingController(rootView: SettingsView(
    25	                viewModel: viewModel
    26	            ))
    27	            window.setFrameAutosaveName("SettingsWindow")
    28	            self.window = window
    29	        }
    30	
    31	        // Refresh the view model on show so launch-at-login status reflects external changes
    32	        Task {
    33	            await viewModel.refresh()
    34	        }
    35	
    36	        NSApp.activate(ignoringOtherApps: true)
    37	        window?.makeKeyAndOrderFront(nil)
    38	    }
    39	}

   273	
   274	    func start() {
   275	        menuBar.install(
   276	            onTogglePause: { [weak self] in self?.paused.toggle(); self?.menuBar.paused = self?.paused ?? false },
   277	            onQuit: { NSApp.terminate(nil) },
   278	            recentApps: { [weak self] in self?.recentApps ?? [] },
   279	            pausedApps: { [weak self] in (try? self?.store.pausedApps()) ?? [] },
   280	            onToggleAppPause: { [weak self] bundleID in
   281	                guard let self else { return }
   282	                let paused = (try? self.store.pausedApps().contains(bundleID)) ?? false
   283	                try? self.store.setAppPaused(bundleID, paused: !paused, nowMs: epochNowMs())
   284	            },
   285	            lastSourceKey: { [weak self] in self?.lastSourceKey },
   286	            onPauseCurrentThread: { [weak self] in
   287	                guard let self, let key = self.lastSourceKey else { return }
   288	                try? self.store.setThreadPaused(key, paused: true, nowMs: epochNowMs())
   289	            },
   290	            onOpenActivity: { [weak self] in self?.activityWindow.show() },
   291	            onOpenPrivacy: { [weak self] in self?.activityPrivacyWindow.show() },
   292	            onOpenSettings: { [weak self] in self?.settingsWindow.show() }
   293	        )
   294	        menuBar.encryptionAvailable = encryptionAvailable
   295	        guard encryptionAvailable else { return }          // capture paused per §9
   296	        do { try store.encryptExistingContent(nowMs: epochNowMs()) }   // §6: backfill before capture
   297	        catch { NSLog("MaxMi: backfill failed, will retry next launch: \(error)") }
   298	
   299	        // Startup crash-repair for activity
   300	        do {
   301	            try store.closeOpenVisits(nowMs: epochNowMs())
   302	            try store.closeOpenSessions(nowMs: epochNowMs())
   303	        } catch {
   304	            NSLog("MaxMi: activity startup crash-repair failed: \(error)")
   305	        }
   306	
   307	        // Show privacy window on first run if consent is unset
   308	        do {
   309	            if try store.activityConsent() == .unset {
   310	                activityPrivacyWindow.show()
   311	            }
   312	        } catch {
   313	            NSLog("MaxMi: failed to check activity consent: \(error)")
   314	        }
   315	
   316	        // Sleep/lock notification for activity
   317	        NSWorkspace.shared.notificationCenter.addObserver(
   318	            forName: NSWorkspace.willSleepNotification,
   319	            object: nil, queue: .main) { [weak self] _ in
   320	            Task { @MainActor [weak self] in
   321	                guard let self else { return }
   322	                let nowMs = epochNowMs()
   323	                try? self.store.closeOpenVisits(nowMs: nowMs)
   324	                self.currentVisitID = nil
   325	                try? self.store.closeActiveSession(nowMs: nowMs)
   326	            }
   327	        }
   328	
   329	        // Screen lock / session resign for activity
   330	        NSWorkspace.shared.notificationCenter.addObserver(
   331	            forName: NSWorkspace.sessionDidResignActiveNotification,
   332	            object: nil, queue: .main) { [weak self] _ in
   333	            Task { @MainActor [weak self] in
   334	                guard let self else { return }
   335	                let nowMs = epochNowMs()
   336	                try? self.store.closeOpenVisits(nowMs: nowMs)
   337	                self.currentVisitID = nil
   338	                try? self.store.closeActiveSession(nowMs: nowMs)
   339	            }
   340	        }
   341	
   342	        guard PermissionGate.ensureAccessibility(menuBar: menuBar) else { return }  // re-checked by menu action
   343	        guard self.observer == nil else { return }  // prevent double-start
   344	        let observer = FocusObserver(
   345	            isCapturable: { [registry] bid in
   346	                // Capture-by-default: every app is capturable EXCEPT sensitive ones (System
   347	                // Settings, password managers, keychain, banking). Browsers and registered
   348	                // parsers always pass; everything else rides the generic fallback unless it's
   349	                // on the sensitive-app denylist. (Was an allowlist — too narrow, missed Cursor/etc.)
   350	                if Browser(rawValue: bid) != nil || registry.parser(for: bid) != nil { return true }
   351	                return !Denylist.isSensitiveApp(bid)
   352	            },
   353	            onCapture: { [weak self] app, pid in
   354	                self?.captureFrontmost(app: app, pid: pid)
   355	            }
   356	        )
   357	        observer.onFocusChanged = { [weak self] app, isCapturable, pid in
   358	            self?.handleFocusChange(app: app, isCapturable: isCapturable, pid: pid)
   359	        }
   360	        observer.start()
   361	        self.observer = observer
   362	        // Pipeline sweep every 30s: picks up idle/frozen versions and due retries (spec §3a sweeper).
   363	        let t = Timer(timeInterval: 30, repeats: true) { [weak self] _ in
   364	            Task { @MainActor in
   365	                guard let self, !self.paused else { return }
   366	                await self.pipeline.tick()
   367	                // Close idle activity sessions (5 min gap)
   368	                _ = try? self.store.closeIdleSessions(idleGapMs: 5*60_000, nowMs: epochNowMs())
   369	                // Summarize due sessions if activity enabled
   370	                if self.isActivitySynthesisEnabled() {
   371	                    await self.displaySummarizer.summarizeDue(nowMs: epochNowMs())
   372	
   373	                    // Trigger agent when enough new summarized sessions exist
   374	                    await self.triggerAgentIfNeeded()
   375	                }
   376	            }
   377	        }
   378	        RunLoop.main.add(t, forMode: .common)
   379	        pipelineTimer = t
   380	
   381	        // Setup hourly background agent scheduler
   382	        setupAgentBackgroundScheduler()
   383	
   384	        // Run agent on launch if overdue (last run > 1h ago)
   385	        Task { @MainActor in
   386	            await self.runAgentIfOverdue()
   387	        }
   388	
   389	        // Meeting capture wiring — guarded by same availability as regular capture
   390	        wireMeetingCapture()
   391	    }
   392	
   393	    private func handleFocusChange(app: AppInfo, isCapturable: Bool, pid: pid_t) {
   394	        let nowMs = epochNowMs()
   395	
   396	        // Bump generation on EVERY focus transition
   397	        focusGeneration += 1
   398	
   399	        // Close active session + all open visits (there should only be one, but closeOpenVisits is the clean approach)
   400	        do {
   401	            try store.closeActiveSession(nowMs: nowMs)
   402	            try store.closeOpenVisits(nowMs: nowMs)
   403	            currentVisitID = nil
   404	        } catch {
   405	            NSLog("MaxMi: activity close failed on focus change: \(error)")
   406	        }
   407	
   408	        // Open new visit ONLY if eligible
   409	        guard isActivityEligible(bundleID: app.bundleID) else { return }
   410	
   500	
   501	        // Ensure whisper model before arming detector
   502	        Task { @MainActor in
   503	            panel.showPreparing()
   504	            do {
   505	                try await modelStore.ensureModel { @Sendable remoteURL in
   506	                    let (tempURL, _) = try await URLSession.shared.download(from: remoteURL)
   507	                    return tempURL
   508	                }
   509	                panel.hidePanel()  // Model ready, hide preparing UI
   510	
   511	                // Now start the detector
   512	                let detector = MeetingDetector()
   513	                self.meetingDetector = detector
   514	
   515	                // Wire detector callbacks
   516	                detector.onCandidate = { [weak session] bundleID, pid in
   517	                    Task {
   518	                        await session?.candidateDetected(bundleID: bundleID, pid: pid, title: nil)
   519	                    }
   520	                }
   521	                detector.onEnded = { [weak session] bundleID in
   522	                    Task {
   523	                        await session?.inputStopped()
   524	                    }
   525	                }
   526	
   527	                detector.start()
   528	            } catch {
   529	                NSLog("MaxMi: whisper model download failed: \(error)")
   530	                panel.showError("Failed to prepare transcription model")
   531	            }
   532	        }
   533	    }
   534	
   535	    func captureFrontmost(app: AppInfo, pid: pid_t) {
   536	        guard !paused else { return }
   537	        // Pause gate: fail closed on DB error (privacy-safe).
   538	        do {
   539	            if try store.pausedApps().contains(app.bundleID) { return }
   540	        } catch {
   541	            NSLog("MaxMi: pausedApps read failed, skipping capture: \(error)")
   542	            return
   543	        }
   544	
   545	        // Track recent apps on attempt (not just commit) so never-committing apps (e.g. WhatsApp shallow tree) can be paused.
   546	        let entry = (bundleID: app.bundleID, name: app.name)
   547	        if !recentApps.contains(where: { $0.bundleID == entry.bundleID }) {
   548	            recentApps.insert(entry, at: 0)
   549	            if recentApps.count > 8 { recentApps.removeLast() }
   550	        }
   551	
   552	        // Capture the current generation for this capture
   553	        let gen = focusGeneration
   554	
   555	        // Chromium browsers and Slack need retry-shortly for post-kick empty trees (spec §10).
   556	        let needsRetry = Browser(rawValue: app.bundleID)?.isChromium == true || app.bundleID == ParserRegistry.slackBundleID
   557	        let attemptsLeft = needsRetry ? 3 : 1
   558	        attemptCapture(app: app, pid: pid, attemptsLeft: attemptsLeft, captureGeneration: gen)
   559	    }
   560	
   561	    private func attemptCapture(app: AppInfo, pid: pid_t, attemptsLeft: Int, captureGeneration: Int) {
   562	        guard !paused else { return }
   563	        // The AX tree read is synchronous cross-process IPC — for heavy trees (Mail ~3600 nodes)
   564	        // it must NOT run on the main thread, or it freezes the menu-bar UI. Read off-main, then
   565	        // resume on the main actor for the DB commit. AXNode is Sendable so the snapshot crosses
   566	        // the actor boundary safely.
   567	        Task.detached(priority: .utility) { [weak self] in
   568	            let snapshot = AXReader.snapshotFrontmostWindow(pid: pid)
   569	            await self?.finishCapture(app: app, pid: pid, attemptsLeft: attemptsLeft, snapshot: snapshot, captureGeneration: captureGeneration)
   570	        }
   571	    }
   572	
   573	    private func finishCapture(app: AppInfo, pid: pid_t, attemptsLeft: Int,
   574	                               snapshot: (window: AXNode, title: String?)?, captureGeneration: Int) {
   575	        guard !paused else { return }
   576	        guard let (window, title) = snapshot else {
   577	            retryOrGiveUp(app: app, pid: pid, attemptsLeft: attemptsLeft, captureGeneration: captureGeneration); return
   578	        }
   579	
   580	        // Build AppInfo with authoritative AXReader title
   581	        let appInfo = AppInfo(bundleID: app.bundleID, name: app.name, windowTitle: title ?? app.windowTitle)
   582	
   583	        do {
   584	            let parsed: ParsedCapture?
   585	
   586	            // Browsers: preserve exact behavior using BrowserTabExtractor
   587	            if Browser(rawValue: app.bundleID) != nil {
   588	                let cap = try BrowserTabExtractor.extract(window: window, windowTitle: title)
   589	                guard !Denylist.isBlockedWebURL(cap.url) else { return }
   590	                // Normalize the URL into a stable thread key so volatile URL state (map coords,
   591	                // tracking params, doc tabs) doesn't fracture one page into many threads.
   592	                let key = URLKeyNormalizer.normalize(cap.url)
   593	                parsed = ParsedCapture(sourceApp: "Web", sourceKey: key, sourceTitle: cap.title, content: cap.content)
   594	            } else {
   595	                // Non-browsers: dispatch through CaptureDispatch
   596	                parsed = CaptureDispatch.parse(window: window, app: appInfo, registry: registry)
   597	            }
   598	
   599	            // Shared tail: guard parsed, check denylist + pause, commit
   600	            guard let parsed else {
   601	                retryOrGiveUp(app: app, pid: pid, attemptsLeft: attemptsLeft, captureGeneration: captureGeneration)
   602	                return
   603	            }
   604	
   605	            // Central keying chokepoint: parsers propose a key; the deriver makes it clean+stable
   606	            // (coarsen-don't-drop). No parser writes the final source_key directly (spec §3a).
   607	            let cleanKey = ThreadKeyDeriver.derive(parsed)
   608	
   609	            // Decision gate: denylist + per-thread pause. Fail closed on DB error.
   610	            let pausedThreads: Set<String>
   611	            do {
   612	                pausedThreads = try store.pausedThreads()
   613	            } catch {
   614	                NSLog("MaxMi: pausedThreads read failed, skipping capture: \(error)")
   615	                return
   616	            }
   617	            guard CaptureDispatch.shouldCommit(parsed: parsed, cleanKey: cleanKey, pausedThreads: pausedThreads) else { return }
   618	            let nowMs = epochNowMs()
   619	            let result = try store.commitCapture(
   620	                CaptureInput(sourceApp: parsed.sourceApp, sourceKey: cleanKey,
   621	                            sourceTitle: parsed.sourceTitle, content: parsed.content),
   622	                nowMs: nowMs)
   623	
   624	            // After normal memory capture commits, record activity evidence ONLY if generation matches AND committed (not deduplicated)
   625	            let eligible = isActivityEligible(bundleID: appInfo.bundleID)
   626	            if MaxMiCore.shouldRecordActivity(captureGeneration: captureGeneration, currentGeneration: focusGeneration, eligible: eligible) {
   627	                // Only record activity for .committed captures (not deduplicated)
   628	                if case .committed(let versionID, _) = result {
   629	                    do {
   630	                        _ = try store.recordActivityCapture(
   631	                            appBundle: appInfo.bundleID,
   632	                            appLabel: appInfo.name,
   633	                            versionID: versionID,
   634	                            content: parsed.content,
   635	                            nowMs: nowMs
   636	                        )
   637	                    } catch {
   638	                        NSLog("MaxMi: activity capture failed: \(error)")
   639	                    }
   640	                }
   641	            }
   642	
   643	            switch result {
   644	            case .committed:
   645	                captureCount += 1
   646	                menuBar.captureCount = captureCount
   647	                lastSourceKey = cleanKey
   648	            case .deduplicated:
   649	                // Update lastSourceKey even on dedup so "Pause current thread" targets the right thread.
   650	                lastSourceKey = cleanKey
   651	            }
   652	        } catch ExtractionError.emptyContent, ExtractionError.noWebArea, ExtractionError.noURL {
   653	            // Browser extraction errors: retry
   654	            retryOrGiveUp(app: app, pid: pid, attemptsLeft: attemptsLeft, captureGeneration: captureGeneration)
   655	        } catch {
   656	            NSLog("MaxMi capture skipped: \(error)")             // logged, skipped, never crash (spec §10)
   657	        }
   658	    }
   659	
   660	    private func retryOrGiveUp(app: AppInfo, pid: pid_t, attemptsLeft: Int, captureGeneration: Int) {
   661	        guard attemptsLeft > 1 else { return }
   662	        DispatchQueue.main.asyncAfter(deadline: .now() + 2) { [weak self] in
   663	            self?.attemptCapture(app: app, pid: pid, attemptsLeft: attemptsLeft - 1, captureGeneration: captureGeneration)
   664	        }
   665	    }
   666	
   667	    // MARK: - Agent Scheduling
   668	
   669	    private func setupAgentBackgroundScheduler() {
   670	        let scheduler = NSBackgroundActivityScheduler(identifier: "com.maxmi.agent.hourly")
   671	        scheduler.interval = 60 * 60  // ~1 hour
   672	        scheduler.tolerance = 10 * 60  // 10 min tolerance
   673	        scheduler.repeats = true
   674	        scheduler.qualityOfService = .utility
   675	
   676	        scheduler.schedule { [weak self] completion in
   677	            Task { @MainActor in
   678	                guard let self else {
   679	                    completion(.finished)
   680	                    return
     1	import AppKit

     3	@MainActor
     4	final class MenuBarController {
     5	    private var statusItem: NSStatusItem?
     6	    private let countItem = NSMenuItem(title: "Captures: 0", action: nil, keyEquivalent: "")
     7	    private let permissionItem = NSMenuItem(title: "⚠ Grant Accessibility…", action: nil, keyEquivalent: "")
     8	    private let keyItem = NSMenuItem(title: "⚠ No GEMINI_API_KEY in .env", action: nil, keyEquivalent: "")
     9	    private let encryptionItem = NSMenuItem(title: "⚠ Memory encryption unavailable", action: nil, keyEquivalent: "")
    10	    private let pauseItem = NSMenuItem(title: "Pause Capture", action: nil, keyEquivalent: "p")
    11	    private var menuDelegate: MenuDelegate?
    12	    private var clickHandler: ClickHandler?
    13	
    14	    var captureCount: Int = 0 { didSet { countItem.title = "Captures: \(captureCount)" } }
    15	    var paused: Bool = false { didSet { pauseItem.title = paused ? "Resume Capture" : "Pause Capture" } }
    16	    var hasAPIKey: Bool = true { didSet { keyItem.isHidden = hasAPIKey } }
    17	    var accessibilityGranted: Bool = true { didSet { permissionItem.isHidden = accessibilityGranted } }
    18	    var encryptionAvailable: Bool = true { didSet { encryptionItem.isHidden = encryptionAvailable } }
    19	
    20	    func install(
    21	        onTogglePause: @escaping () -> Void,
    22	        onQuit: @escaping () -> Void,
    23	        recentApps: @escaping () -> [(bundleID: String, name: String)],
    24	        pausedApps: @escaping () -> Set<String>,
    25	        onToggleAppPause: @escaping (String) -> Void,
    26	        lastSourceKey: @escaping () -> String?,
    27	        onPauseCurrentThread: @escaping () -> Void,
    28	        onOpenActivity: @escaping () -> Void,
    29	        onOpenPrivacy: @escaping () -> Void,
    30	        onOpenSettings: @escaping () -> Void
    31	    ) {
    32	        guard statusItem == nil else { return }
    33	        let item = NSStatusBar.system.statusItem(withLength: NSStatusItem.variableLength)
    34	
    35	        // Set dog icon from bundle
    36	        if let imageURL = Bundle.main.url(forResource: "tray-dog", withExtension: "png"),
    37	           let image = NSImage(contentsOf: imageURL) {
    38	            image.isTemplate = true
    39	            item.button?.image = image
    40	        }
    41	
    42	        let menu = NSMenu()
    43	
    44	        // Activity menu items
    45	        let openActivityItem = NSMenuItem(title: "Open MaxMi", action: nil, keyEquivalent: "")
    46	        openActivityItem.setAction { onOpenActivity() }
    47	        menu.addItem(openActivityItem)
    48	
    49	        let privacyItem = NSMenuItem(title: "Activity Privacy…", action: nil, keyEquivalent: "")
    50	        privacyItem.setAction { onOpenPrivacy() }
    51	        menu.addItem(privacyItem)
    52	
    53	        let settingsItem = NSMenuItem(title: "Settings…", action: nil, keyEquivalent: ",")
    54	        settingsItem.setAction { onOpenSettings() }
    55	        menu.addItem(settingsItem)
    56	
    57	        menu.addItem(.separator())
    58	
    59	        permissionItem.isHidden = accessibilityGranted
    60	        keyItem.isHidden = hasAPIKey
    61	        encryptionItem.isHidden = encryptionAvailable
    62	        permissionItem.action = #selector(NSApplication.openAccessibilitySettings)
    63	        permissionItem.target = NSApp
    64	        menu.addItem(countItem)
    65	        menu.addItem(.separator())
    66	        menu.addItem(permissionItem)
    67	        menu.addItem(keyItem)
    68	        menu.addItem(encryptionItem)
    69	        menu.addItem(pauseItem)
    70	        pauseItem.setAction { onTogglePause() }
    71	
    72	        // Per-app pause submenu
    73	        let appPauseItem = NSMenuItem(title: "Pause capture for ▸", action: nil, keyEquivalent: "")
    74	        let appPauseMenu = NSMenu()
    75	        appPauseItem.submenu = appPauseMenu
    76	
    77	        // Pause current thread
    78	        let pauseThreadItem = NSMenuItem(title: "Pause capture for current thread", action: nil, keyEquivalent: "")
    79	        pauseThreadItem.setAction(onPauseCurrentThread)
    80	
    81	        // Populate dynamically on menu open
    82	        let delegate = MenuDelegate(
    83	            updateAppPauseMenu: { [weak appPauseMenu] in
    84	                guard let appPauseMenu else { return }
    85	                appPauseMenu.removeAllItems()
    86	                let recent = recentApps()
    87	                let paused = pausedApps()
    88	                for app in recent {
    89	                    let item = NSMenuItem(title: app.name, action: nil, keyEquivalent: "")
    90	                    item.state = paused.contains(app.bundleID) ? .on : .off
    91	                    item.setAction { onToggleAppPause(app.bundleID) }
    92	                    appPauseMenu.addItem(item)
    93	                }
    94	                if recent.isEmpty {
    95	                    let placeholder = NSMenuItem(title: "No recent apps", action: nil, keyEquivalent: "")
    96	                    placeholder.isEnabled = false
    97	                    appPauseMenu.addItem(placeholder)
    98	                }
    99	            },
   100	            updatePauseThreadItem: { [weak pauseThreadItem] in
   101	                pauseThreadItem?.isEnabled = lastSourceKey() != nil
   102	            }
   103	        )
   104	        self.menuDelegate = delegate
   105	        menu.delegate = delegate
   106	        menu.addItem(appPauseItem)
   107	        menu.addItem(pauseThreadItem)
   108	
   109	        menu.addItem(.separator())
   110	        let quit = NSMenuItem(title: "Quit MaxMi", action: nil, keyEquivalent: "q")
   111	        quit.setAction { onQuit() }
   112	        menu.addItem(quit)
   113	
   114	        // Install click handler: statusItem.menu stays nil; we popUpMenu directly on right-click
   115	        statusItem = item
   116	        if let button = item.button {
   117	            button.sendAction(on: [.leftMouseUp, .rightMouseUp])
   118	            let handler = ClickHandler(
   119	                onLeftClick: { onOpenActivity() },
   120	                onRightClick: { @MainActor [weak item] in
   121	                    guard let item else { return }
   122	                    item.popUpMenu(menu)
   123	                }
   124	            )
   125	            self.clickHandler = handler
   126	            button.target = handler
   127	            button.action = #selector(ClickHandler.handleClick)
   128	        }
   129	    }
   130	}
   131	
   132	// Closure-backed NSMenuItem actions (no @objc target boilerplate per item).
   133	private final class ActionTrampoline: NSObject {
   134	    let block: () -> Void
   135	    init(_ block: @escaping () -> Void) { self.block = block }
   136	    @objc func fire() { block() }
   137	}
   138	private let trampolineKey: StaticString = "trampolineKey"
   139	extension NSMenuItem {
   140	    func setAction(_ block: @escaping () -> Void) {
   141	        let t = ActionTrampoline(block)
   142	        objc_setAssociatedObject(self, trampolineKey.utf8Start, t, .OBJC_ASSOCIATION_RETAIN)
   143	        target = t
   144	        action = #selector(ActionTrampoline.fire)
   145	    }
   146	}
   147	extension NSApplication {
   148	    @objc func openAccessibilitySettings() {
   149	        NSWorkspace.shared.open(URL(string:
   150	            "x-apple.systempreferences:com.apple.preference.security?Privacy_Accessibility")!)
   151	    }
   152	}
   153	
   154	private final class MenuDelegate: NSObject, NSMenuDelegate {
   155	    let updateAppPauseMenu: () -> Void
   156	    let updatePauseThreadItem: () -> Void
   157	    init(updateAppPauseMenu: @escaping () -> Void, updatePauseThreadItem: @escaping () -> Void) {
   158	        self.updateAppPauseMenu = updateAppPauseMenu
   159	        self.updatePauseThreadItem = updatePauseThreadItem
   160	    }
   161	    func menuWillOpen(_ menu: NSMenu) {
   162	        updateAppPauseMenu()
   163	        updatePauseThreadItem()
   164	    }
   165	}
   166	
   167	@MainActor
   168	private final class ClickHandler: NSObject {
   169	    let onLeftClick: () -> Void
   170	    let onRightClick: () -> Void
   171	
   172	    init(onLeftClick: @escaping () -> Void, onRightClick: @escaping () -> Void) {
   173	        self.onLeftClick = onLeftClick
   174	        self.onRightClick = onRightClick
   175	    }
   176	
   177	    @objc func handleClick() {
   178	        guard let event = NSApp.currentEvent else { return }
   179	        switch event.type {
   180	        case .leftMouseUp:
   181	            onLeftClick()
   182	        case .rightMouseUp:
   183	            onRightClick()
   184	        default:
   185	            break
   186	        }
   187	    }
   188	}

     1	import XCTest
     2	import GRDB
     3	@testable import MaxMiStore
     4	import MaxMiCore

     6	final class ActivityStoreTests: XCTestCase {
     7	    var store: Store!
     8	    var db: MaxMiDatabase!
     9	    override func setUpWithError() throws {
    10	        db = try .inMemory()
    11	        store = Store(db: db, cipher: AESGCMFieldCipher.testCipher)
    12	    }
    13	    let t0 = EpochMs(496_000) * 3_600_000
    14	
    15	    func testEvidenceEncryptedAndCoalesced() throws {
    16	        let s = try store.recordActivityCapture(appBundle: "com.x", appLabel: "X", versionID: nil, content: "did a thing", nowMs: t0)
    17	        let s2 = try store.recordActivityCapture(appBundle: "com.x", appLabel: "X", versionID: nil, content: "did a thing", nowMs: t0+1000)
    18	        XCTAssertEqual(s, s2)
    19	        try db.dbQueue.read { d in
    20	            let rows = try Row.fetchAll(d, sql: "SELECT content_ciphertext FROM activity_session_evidence WHERE session_id=?", arguments: [s])
    21	            XCTAssertEqual(rows.count, 1, "duplicate content coalesced")
    22	            XCTAssertTrue((rows[0]["content_ciphertext"] as String).hasPrefix("enc:v1:"))
    23	        }
    24	        XCTAssertEqual(try store.sessionEvidence(s), ["did a thing"])
    25	    }
    26	
    27	    func testCloseAndSummarizeWithStaleGuard() throws {
    28	        let s = try store.recordActivityCapture(appBundle: "com.x", appLabel: "X", versionID: nil, content: "wrote the parser", nowMs: t0)
    29	        try store.closeSession(s, nowMs: t0+60_000)
    30	        let h = try store.sessionSourceHash(s)
    31	        XCTAssertTrue(try store.setSessionSummary(s, summary: "Worked on the parser", expectedSourceHash: h, modelID: "gemini-2.5-flash-lite", promptVersion: "v1", nowMs: t0+61_000))
    32	        XCTAssertFalse(try store.setSessionSummary(s, summary: "stale", expectedSourceHash: "WRONGHASH", modelID: "m", promptVersion: "v1", nowMs: t0+62_000), "stale hash must no-op")
    33	        let recent = try store.recentSessions(limit: 10)
    34	        XCTAssertEqual(recent.first?.summary, "Worked on the parser")
    35	        XCTAssertEqual(recent.first?.summaryStatus, "summarized")
    36	    }
    37	
    38	    func testDeleteActivityForAppCascades() throws {
    39	        let s = try store.recordActivityCapture(appBundle: "com.secret", appLabel: "S", versionID: nil, content: "x", nowMs: t0)
    40	        try store.closeActiveSession(nowMs: t0+1)
    41	        try store.deleteActivityForApp("com.secret")
    42	        try db.dbQueue.read { d in
    43	            XCTAssertEqual(try Int.fetchOne(d, sql: "SELECT count(*) FROM activity_sessions WHERE app_bundle='com.secret'"), 0)
    44	            XCTAssertEqual(try Int.fetchOne(d, sql: "SELECT count(*) FROM activity_session_evidence"), 0, "evidence cascade-deleted")
    45	        }
    46	    }
    47	
    48	    func testCrashRepairClosesDanglingVisits() throws {
    49	        _ = try store.openVisit(appBundle: "com.x", appLabel: "X", nowMs: t0)
    50	        try store.closeOpenVisits(nowMs: t0+5000)
    51	        try db.dbQueue.read { d in
    52	            XCTAssertEqual(try Int.fetchOne(d, sql: "SELECT count(*) FROM activity_app_visits WHERE ended_at IS NULL"), 0)
    53	        }
    54	    }

    56	    func testObservedActivityApps() throws {
    57	        // Record sessions for multiple apps
    58	        let s1 = try store.recordActivityCapture(appBundle: "com.apple.Safari", appLabel: "Safari", versionID: nil, content: "browsing", nowMs: t0)
    59	        try store.closeSession(s1, nowMs: t0+1000)
    60	        let s2 = try store.recordActivityCapture(appBundle: "com.microsoft.VSCode", appLabel: "Visual Studio Code", versionID: nil, content: "coding", nowMs: t0+2000)
    61	        try store.closeSession(s2, nowMs: t0+3000)
    62	        // Same app again with updated label (most recent should win)
    63	        let s3 = try store.recordActivityCapture(appBundle: "com.apple.Safari", appLabel: "Safari (Updated)", versionID: nil, content: "more browsing", nowMs: t0+4000)
    64	        try store.closeSession(s3, nowMs: t0+5000)
    65	
    66	        let apps = try store.observedActivityApps()
    67	        XCTAssertEqual(apps.count, 2, "two distinct apps")
    68	
    69	        // Check Safari has updated label
    70	        let safari = apps.first { $0.bundle == "com.apple.Safari" }
    71	        XCTAssertEqual(safari?.label, "Safari (Updated)", "most recent label")
    72	
    73	        // Check VSCode
    74	        let vscode = apps.first { $0.bundle == "com.microsoft.VSCode" }
    75	        XCTAssertEqual(vscode?.label, "Visual Studio Code")
    76	    }
    77	}

     7	    func testRefreshPopulatesFields() async {
     8	        let snapshot = SettingsSnapshot(
     9	            launchAtLoginStatus: .notRegistered,
    10	            activityEnabled: true,
    11	            consentGranted: true,
    12	            excludedApps: [
    13	                SettingsExcludedApp(id: "com.apple.Safari", name: "Safari", excluded: false),
    14	                SettingsExcludedApp(id: "com.microsoft.VSCode", name: "Visual Studio Code", excluded: true)
    15	            ],
    16	            version: "1.0",
    17	            statusLines: ["Accessibility: Granted", "API Key: Configured"]
    18	        )
    19	
    20	        let vm = SettingsViewModel(
    21	            load: { snapshot },
    22	            onSetLaunchAtLogin: { _ in },
    23	            onSetActivityEnabled: { _ in },
    24	            onToggleExcluded: { _, _ in },
    25	            onCheckUpdates: { "Checking updates is manual" }
    26	        )
    27	
    28	        await vm.refresh()
    29	
    30	        XCTAssertEqual(vm.launchAtLoginStatus, .notRegistered)
    31	        XCTAssertEqual(vm.activityEnabled, true)
    32	        XCTAssertEqual(vm.consentGranted, true)
    33	        XCTAssertEqual(vm.excludedApps.count, 2)
    34	        XCTAssertEqual(vm.excludedApps[0].id, "com.apple.Safari")
    35	        XCTAssertEqual(vm.excludedApps[0].excluded, false)
    36	        XCTAssertEqual(vm.excludedApps[1].id, "com.microsoft.VSCode")
    37	        XCTAssertEqual(vm.excludedApps[1].excluded, true)
    38	        XCTAssertEqual(vm.version, "1.0")
    39	        XCTAssertEqual(vm.statusLines, ["Accessibility: Granted", "API Key: Configured"])
    40	    }

    42	    func testToggleExcludedCallsClosureAndReloads() async {
    43	        nonisolated(unsafe) var toggledBundle: String?
    44	        nonisolated(unsafe) var toggledExcluded: Bool?
    45	        nonisolated(unsafe) var loadCount = 0
    46	
    47	        let initialSnapshot = SettingsSnapshot(
    48	            launchAtLoginStatus: .notRegistered,
    49	            activityEnabled: true,
    50	            consentGranted: true,
    51	            excludedApps: [
    52	                SettingsExcludedApp(id: "com.app", name: "App", excluded: false)
    53	            ],
    54	            version: "1.0",
    55	            statusLines: []
    56	        )
    57	
    58	        let updatedSnapshot = SettingsSnapshot(
    59	            launchAtLoginStatus: .notRegistered,
    60	            activityEnabled: true,
    61	            consentGranted: true,
    62	            excludedApps: [
    63	                SettingsExcludedApp(id: "com.app", name: "App", excluded: true)
    64	            ],
    65	            version: "1.0",
    66	            statusLines: []
    67	        )
    68	
    69	        let vm = SettingsViewModel(
    70	            load: {
    71	                loadCount += 1
    72	                return loadCount == 1 ? initialSnapshot : updatedSnapshot
    73	            },
    74	            onSetLaunchAtLogin: { _ in },
    75	            onSetActivityEnabled: { _ in },
    76	            onToggleExcluded: { bundle, excluded in
    77	                toggledBundle = bundle
    78	                toggledExcluded = excluded
    79	            },
    80	            onCheckUpdates: { "Manual" }
    81	        )
    82	
    83	        await vm.refresh()
    84	        XCTAssertEqual(loadCount, 1)
    85	        XCTAssertEqual(vm.excludedApps.first?.excluded, false)
    86	
    87	        await vm.toggleExcluded("com.app")
    88	
    89	        XCTAssertEqual(toggledBundle, "com.app")
    90	        XCTAssertEqual(toggledExcluded, true, "should toggle from false to true")
    91	        XCTAssertEqual(loadCount, 2, "reload after toggle")
    92	        XCTAssertEqual(vm.excludedApps.first?.excluded, true)
    93	    }

   183	        await vm.refresh()
   184	        XCTAssertEqual(vm.consentGranted, false)
   185	
   186	        // Attempt to enable activity when consent is not granted
   187	        vm.activityEnabled = true
   188	
   189	        // The view model should reject this change (consent gating)
   190	        // In the real UI, the toggle would be disabled, but we verify the setter behavior
   191	        XCTAssertEqual(setEnabledCalls.count, 1, "setter should call closure")
   192	    }
   193	
   194	    func testActivityEnabledSetterCallsOnSetActivityEnabled() async {
   195	        nonisolated(unsafe) var setCalls: [Bool] = []
   196	        let vm = SettingsViewModel(
   197	            load: {
   198	                SettingsSnapshot(
   199	                    launchAtLoginStatus: .notRegistered,
   200	                    activityEnabled: false,
   201	                    consentGranted: true,
   202	                    excludedApps: [],
   203	                    version: "1.0",
   204	                    statusLines: []
   205	                )
   206	            },
   207	            onSetLaunchAtLogin: { _ in },
   208	            onSetActivityEnabled: { enabled in
   209	                setCalls.append(enabled)
   210	            },
   211	            onToggleExcluded: { _, _ in },
   212	            onCheckUpdates: { "Manual" }
   213	        )
   214	
   215	        await vm.refresh()
   216	
   217	        vm.activityEnabled = true
   218	        XCTAssertEqual(setCalls, [true])
   219	
   220	        vm.activityEnabled = false
   221	        XCTAssertEqual(setCalls, [true, false])
   222	    }
   223	}

     1	import Foundation
     2	import MaxMiCore
     3	import Observation
     4	
     5	@MainActor
     6	@Observable
     7	public final class ActivityViewModel {
     8	    public private(set) var groups: [(day: String, rows: [SessionRow])] = []
     9	
    10	    private let load: @Sendable () async -> [TimelineSessionDTO]
    11	    private let now: () -> Int64
    12	
    13	    public init(load: @escaping @Sendable () async -> [TimelineSessionDTO], now: @escaping () -> Int64) {
    14	        self.load = load
    15	        self.now = now
    16	    }
    17	
    18	    public func refresh() async {
    19	        let dtos = await load()
    20	        let nowMs = now()
    21	
    22	        // Map DTOs to rows with precomputed display fields
    23	        let rows = dtos.map { dto in
    24	            SessionRow(
    25	                id: dto.id,
    26	                appLabel: dto.appLabel,
    27	                timeAgo: formatTimeAgo(startedAtMs: dto.startedAtMs, nowMs: nowMs),
    28	                dayGroup: dayGroupLabel(startedAtMs: dto.startedAtMs, nowMs: nowMs),
    29	                summary: dto.summary ?? "Activity in \(dto.appLabel)",
    30	                evidence: dto.evidence
    31	            )
    32	        }
    33	
    34	        // Sort by startedAtMs descending (newest first)
    35	        let sorted = rows.sorted { lhs, rhs in
    36	            let lhsMs = dtos.first(where: { $0.id == lhs.id })?.startedAtMs ?? 0
    37	            let rhsMs = dtos.first(where: { $0.id == rhs.id })?.startedAtMs ?? 0
    38	            return lhsMs > rhsMs
    39	        }
    40	
    41	        // Group by day
    42	        var grouped: [String: [SessionRow]] = [:]
    43	        for row in sorted {
    44	            grouped[row.dayGroup, default: []].append(row)
    45	        }
    46	
    47	        // Sort groups: Today, Yesterday, then dates
    48	        let groupOrder = ["Today", "Yesterday"]
    49	        let sortedGroups = grouped.sorted { lhs, rhs in
    50	            if let lhsIndex = groupOrder.firstIndex(of: lhs.key) {
    51	                if let rhsIndex = groupOrder.firstIndex(of: rhs.key) {
    52	                    return lhsIndex < rhsIndex
    53	                }
    54	                return true
    55	            }
    56	            if groupOrder.contains(rhs.key) {
    57	                return false
    58	            }
    59	            return lhs.key > rhs.key
    60	        }
    61	
    62	        groups = sortedGroups.map { (day: $0.key, rows: $0.value) }
    63	    }
    64	
    65	    private func formatTimeAgo(startedAtMs: EpochMs, nowMs: EpochMs) -> String {
    66	        let deltaMs = nowMs - startedAtMs
    67	        let minutes = deltaMs / 60_000
    68	        let hours = deltaMs / 3_600_000
    69	
    70	        if minutes < 60 {
    71	            return "\(minutes)m ago"
    72	        } else {
    73	            return "\(hours)h ago"
    74	        }
    75	    }
    76	
    77	    private func dayGroupLabel(startedAtMs: EpochMs, nowMs: EpochMs) -> String {
    78	        let calendar = Calendar.current
    79	        let startDate = Date(timeIntervalSince1970: Double(startedAtMs) / 1000.0)
    80	        let nowDate = Date(timeIntervalSince1970: Double(nowMs) / 1000.0)
    81	
    82	        let startDay = calendar.startOfDay(for: startDate)
    83	        let nowDay = calendar.startOfDay(for: nowDate)
    84	
    85	        let dayDiff = calendar.dateComponents([.day], from: startDay, to: nowDay).day ?? 0
    86	
    87	        switch dayDiff {
    88	        case 0:
    89	            return "Today"
    90	        case 1:
    91	            return "Yesterday"
    92	        default:
    93	            let formatter = DateFormatter()
    94	            formatter.dateStyle = .medium
    95	            formatter.timeStyle = .none
    96	            return formatter.string(from: startDate)
    97	        }
    98	    }
    99	}

     4	@MainActor
     5	@Observable
     6	public final class ActionItemsViewModel {
     7	    public private(set) var open: [ActionItemDTO] = []
     8	    public private(set) var archived: [ActionItemDTO] = []
     9	
    10	    private let load: @Sendable () async -> (open: [ActionItemDTO], archived: [ActionItemDTO])
    11	    private let onResolve: @Sendable (String) async throws -> Void
    12	    private let onDismiss: @Sendable (String) async throws -> Void
    13	
    14	    public init(
    15	        load: @escaping @Sendable () async -> (open: [ActionItemDTO], archived: [ActionItemDTO]),
    16	        onResolve: @escaping @Sendable (String) async throws -> Void,
    17	        onDismiss: @escaping @Sendable (String) async throws -> Void
    18	    ) {
    19	        self.load = load
    20	        self.onResolve = onResolve
    21	        self.onDismiss = onDismiss
    22	    }
    23	
    24	    public func refresh() async {
    25	        let result = await load()
    26	        self.open = result.open
    27	        self.archived = result.archived
    28	    }
    29	
    30	    public func resolve(_ id: String) async {
    31	        do {
    32	            try await onResolve(id)
    33	            // Refresh only on success
    34	            await refresh()
    35	        } catch {
    36	            // On failure, keep the item (don't refresh)
    37	        }
    38	    }
    39	
    40	    public func dismiss(_ id: String) async {
    41	        do {
    42	            try await onDismiss(id)
    43	            // Refresh only on success
    44	            await refresh()
    45	        } catch {
    46	            // On failure, keep the item (don't refresh)
    47	        }
    48	    }
    49	}

   413	            }
   414	        }
   415	    }

   425	        let minutes = elapsed / 60

   427	        timerLabel?.stringValue = String(format: "%02d:%02d", minutes, seconds)
   428	    }

     1	import AppKit
     2	import SwiftUI
     3	import MaxMiCore
     4	import MaxMiStore
     5	
     6	@MainActor
     7	final class ActivityPrivacyWindow: NSObject, NSWindowDelegate {
     8	    private var window: NSWindow?
     9	    private let store: Store
    10	
    11	    init(store: Store) {
    12	        self.store = store
    13	        super.init()
    14	    }
    15	
    16	    func show() {
    17	        if window == nil {
    18	            let window = NSWindow(
    19	                contentRect: NSRect(x: 0, y: 0, width: 500, height: 600),
    20	                styleMask: [.titled, .closable],
    21	                backing: .buffered,
    22	                defer: false
    23	            )
    24	            window.title = "Activity Privacy"
    25	            window.center()
    26	            let contentView = ActivityPrivacyView(store: store)
    27	            window.contentViewController = NSHostingController(rootView: contentView)
    28	            window.setFrameAutosaveName("ActivityPrivacyWindow")
    29	            window.delegate = self
    30	            self.window = window
    31	        }
    32	
    33	        NSApp.activate(ignoringOtherApps: true)
    34	        window?.makeKeyAndOrderFront(nil)
    35	    }
    36	
    37	    nonisolated func windowWillClose(_ notification: Notification) {
    38	        // When the privacy window closes and consent is still unset, persist .declined
    39	        Task { @MainActor in
    40	            do {
    41	                let consent = try store.activityConsent()
    42	                if consent == .unset {
    43	                    try store.setActivityConsent(.declined)
    44	                }
    45	            } catch {
    46	                NSLog("MaxMi: failed to persist declined consent on window close: \(error)")
    47	            }
    48	        }
    49	    }
    50	}
    51	
    52	// MARK: - SwiftUI Content
    53	
    54	private struct ActivityPrivacyView: View {
    55	    let store: Store
    56	    @State private var enabled: Bool = false
    57	    @State private var excludedApps: Set<String> = []
    58	    @State private var recentApps: [(bundleID: String, label: String)] = []
    59	
    60	    var body: some View {
    61	        ScrollView {
    62	            VStack(alignment: .leading, spacing: 24) {
    63	                // Consent disclosure
    64	                VStack(alignment: .leading, spacing: 12) {
    65	                    Text("Activity Synthesis")
    66	                        .font(.title2.bold())
    67	
    68	                    Text("""
    69	                        MaxMi can synthesize your Mac activity into a timeline using Gemini AI. Screen content will be:
    70	                        • Encrypted locally before processing
    71	                        • Sent to Google's Gemini API for processing
    72	                        • Subject to Google's Gemini API data use policies
    73	
    74	                        You can exclude specific apps and disable this feature at any time.
    75	                        """)
    76	                        .font(.body)
    77	                        .foregroundColor(.secondary)
    78	                }
    79	                .padding()
    80	                .background(Color(NSColor.controlBackgroundColor))
    81	                .cornerRadius(8)
    82	
    83	                // Global enable toggle
    84	                Toggle("Enable activity synthesis", isOn: $enabled)
    85	                    .padding()
    86	                    .background(Color(NSColor.controlBackgroundColor))
    87	                    .cornerRadius(8)
    88	                    .onChange(of: enabled) { oldValue, newValue in
    89	                        handleEnableToggle(newValue)
    90	                    }
    91	
    92	                // Per-app exclusion list
    93	                if enabled {
    94	                    VStack(alignment: .leading, spacing: 12) {
    95	                        Text("App Exclusions")
    96	                            .font(.headline)
    97	
    98	                        if recentApps.isEmpty {
    99	                            Text("No apps to exclude yet. Use your Mac to see apps here.")
   100	                                .font(.caption)
   101	                                .foregroundColor(.secondary)
   102	                                .padding()
   103	                        } else {
   104	                            ForEach(recentApps, id: \.bundleID) { app in
   105	                                Toggle(app.label, isOn: Binding(
   106	                                    get: { !excludedApps.contains(app.bundleID) },
   107	                                    set: { included in
   108	                                        handleAppToggle(bundleID: app.bundleID, included: included)
   109	                                    }
   110	                                ))
   111	                            }
   112	                        }
   113	                    }
   114	                    .padding()
   115	                    .background(Color(NSColor.controlBackgroundColor))
   116	                    .cornerRadius(8)
   117	                }
   118	
   119	                Spacer()
   120	            }
   121	            .padding()
   122	        }
   123	        .frame(minWidth: 500, minHeight: 600)
   124	        .onAppear {
   125	            loadState()
   126	        }
   127	    }
   128	
   129	    private func loadState() {
   130	        do {
   131	            let consent = try store.activityConsent()
   132	            let activityEnabled = try store.activityEnabled()
   133	            enabled = consent == .granted && activityEnabled
   134	            excludedApps = try store.activityExcludedApps()
   135	
   136	            // Load recent apps from activity sessions
   137	            let sessions = try store.recentSessions(limit: 50)
   138	            var seen: Set<String> = []
   139	            var apps: [(String, String)] = []
   140	            for session in sessions {
   141	                if !seen.contains(session.appBundle) {
   142	                    apps.append((session.appBundle, session.appLabel))
   143	                    seen.insert(session.appBundle)
   144	                }
   145	            }
   146	            recentApps = apps
   147	        } catch {
   148	            NSLog("MaxMi: failed to load activity privacy state: \(error)")
   149	        }
   150	    }
   151	
   152	    private func handleEnableToggle(_ newValue: Bool) {
   153	        do {
   154	            if newValue {
   155	                // First enable: set consent to granted
   156	                let consent = try store.activityConsent()
   157	                if consent == .unset {
   158	                    try store.setActivityConsent(.granted)
   159	                }
   160	                try store.setActivityEnabled(true)
   161	            } else {
   162	                // Disable: close active sessions/visits and persist the disable
   163	                let nowMs = epochNowMs()
   164	                try store.closeOpenVisits(nowMs: nowMs)
   165	                try store.closeActiveSession(nowMs: nowMs)
   166	
   167	                let consent = try store.activityConsent()
   168	                if consent == .unset {
   169	                    try store.setActivityConsent(.declined)
   170	                }
   171	                try store.setActivityEnabled(false)
   172	            }
   173	        } catch {
   174	            NSLog("MaxMi: failed to update activity enabled state: \(error)")
   175	        }
   176	    }
   177	
   178	    private func handleAppToggle(bundleID: String, included: Bool) {
   179	        do {
   180	            let excluded = !included
   181	            try store.setActivityExcluded(bundleID, excluded)
   182	            if excluded {
   183	                try store.deleteActivityForApp(bundleID)
   184	                // Refresh the recent apps list
   185	                loadState()
   186	            }
   187	
   188	            // Update local state
   189	            if excluded {
   190	                excludedApps.insert(bundleID)
   191	            } else {
   192	                excludedApps.remove(bundleID)
   193	            }
   194	        } catch {
   195	            NSLog("MaxMi: failed to update app exclusion: \(error)")
   196	        }
   197	    }
   198	}

     1	import Foundation
     2	import GRDB
     3	import CSQLiteVec
     4	
     5	public final class MaxMiDatabase {
     6	    public let dbQueue: DatabaseQueue
     7	
     8	    public init(path: String, readOnly: Bool = false) throws {
     9	        var config = Configuration()
    10	        config.readonly = readOnly
    11	        config.prepareDatabase { db in
    12	            try db.execute(sql: "PRAGMA foreign_keys = ON")
    13	            var err: UnsafeMutablePointer<CChar>? = nil
    14	            let rc = sqlite3_vec_init(db.sqliteConnection, &err, nil)
    15	            if rc != SQLITE_OK {
    16	                let msg = err.map { String(cString: $0) } ?? "sqlite3_vec_init failed"
    17	                sqlite3_free(err)
    18	                throw DatabaseError(resultCode: ResultCode(rawValue: rc), message: msg)
    19	            }
    20	        }
    21	        let isFile = path != ":memory:"
    22	        if isFile && !readOnly {
    23	            try FileManager.default.createDirectory(
    24	                at: URL(fileURLWithPath: path).deletingLastPathComponent(),
    25	                withIntermediateDirectories: true)
    26	        }
    27	        dbQueue = try DatabaseQueue(path: path, configuration: config)
    28	        if isFile && !readOnly {
    29	            // Must be outside transaction (GRDB starts a deferred transaction in .write).
    30	            try dbQueue.inDatabase { db in
    31	                try db.execute(sql: "PRAGMA journal_mode = WAL")
    32	            }
    33	            for suffix in ["", "-wal", "-shm"] {
    34	                try? FileManager.default.setAttributes(
    35	                    [.posixPermissions: 0o600], ofItemAtPath: path + suffix)
    36	            }
    37	        }
    38	        if !readOnly {
    39	            try Migrations.migrator.migrate(dbQueue)
    40	        }
    41	    }
    42	
    43	    public static func inMemory() throws -> MaxMiDatabase {
    44	        try MaxMiDatabase(path: ":memory:")
    45	    }
    46	}

     5	public struct CaptureInput: Sendable {
     6	    public let sourceApp: String
     7	    public let sourceKey: String
     8	    public let sourceTitle: String?
     9	    public let content: String
    10	    public init(sourceApp: String, sourceKey: String, sourceTitle: String?, content: String) {
    11	        self.sourceApp = sourceApp; self.sourceKey = sourceKey
    12	        self.sourceTitle = sourceTitle; self.content = content
    13	    }
    14	}
    15	
    16	public enum CommitResult: Equatable, Sendable {
    17	    case deduplicated
    18	    case committed(versionID: String, contentHash: String)
    19	}
    20	
    21	public final class Store {
    22	    let db: MaxMiDatabase
    23	    let cipher: any FieldCipher
    24	    public init(db: MaxMiDatabase, cipher: any FieldCipher) {
    25	        self.db = db; self.cipher = cipher
    26	    }
    27	
    28	    /// Decrypt for reads; integrity/malformed failures become a marker, never a throw.
    29	    func decryptOrMarker(_ stored: String) -> String {
    30	        (try? cipher.decrypt(stored)) ?? "[unreadable memory]"
    31	    }
    32	
    33	    /// Split content into items, fingerprint each (normalized), record novel ones.
    34	    /// Returns true if ANY item was novel (=> commit). Fails OPEN (true) on error (spec §7).
    35	    private func recordNovelFingerprints(_ content: String, threadID: String, nowMs: EpochMs,
    36	                                         _ d: Database) -> Bool {
    37	        // Items = non-empty lines (chat/mail/terminal); a single-line/document is one item.
    38	        let items = content.split(separator: "\n").map {
    39	            $0.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespaces).lowercased()
    40	        }.filter { !$0.isEmpty }
    41	        guard !items.isEmpty else { return true }
    42	        var anyNovel = false
    43	        for item in items {
    44	            let fp = ContentHash.sha256Hex("\(threadID)\n\(item)")   // thread-scoped fingerprint
    45	            do {
    46	                let exists = try Int.fetchOne(d, sql:
    47	                    "SELECT 1 FROM message_fingerprints WHERE fingerprint=? LIMIT 1", arguments: [fp]) != nil
    48	                if !exists {
    49	                    anyNovel = true
    50	                    try d.execute(sql: "INSERT OR IGNORE INTO message_fingerprints (fingerprint, thread_id, seen_at) VALUES (?,?,?)",
    51	                                  arguments: [fp, threadID, nowMs])
    52	                }
    53	            } catch {
    54	                return true   // fail open: never lose a capture over a dedup error
    55	            }
    56	        }
    57	        return anyNovel
    58	    }
    59	
    60	    public func commitCapture(_ input: CaptureInput, nowMs: EpochMs) throws -> CommitResult {
    61	        let hash = ContentHash.sha256Hex(input.content)
    62	        let bucket = HourBucket.bucket(forMs: nowMs)
    63	        let words = input.content.split(whereSeparator: \.isWhitespace).count
    64	        let storedContent = try cipher.encrypt(input.content)
    65	
    66	        return try db.dbQueue.write { d in
    67	            // 1. Upsert thread; dedup on unchanged tree hash.
    68	            let existing = try Row.fetchOne(d,
    69	                sql: "SELECT id, last_tree_hash FROM threads WHERE source_app=? AND source_key=?",
    70	                arguments: [input.sourceApp, input.sourceKey])
    71	            let threadID: String
    72	            if let existing {
    73	                if existing["last_tree_hash"] as String? == hash { return .deduplicated }
    74	                threadID = existing["id"]
    75	                try d.execute(sql: "UPDATE threads SET source_title=?, last_tree_hash=?, updated_at=? WHERE id=?",
    76	                              arguments: [input.sourceTitle, hash, nowMs, threadID])
    77	            } else {
    78	                threadID = Ident.uuidv7(nowMs: nowMs)
    79	                try d.execute(sql: """
    80	                    INSERT INTO threads (id, source_app, source_key, source_title, last_tree_hash, created_at, updated_at)
    81	                    VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?)
    82	                    """, arguments: [threadID, input.sourceApp, input.sourceKey, input.sourceTitle, hash, nowMs, nowMs])
    83	            }
    84	
    85	            // Per-item fingerprint dedup: if no line is novel for this thread, skip (spec §3b).
    86	            // Complements last_tree_hash (which catches identical whole trees) by catching
    87	            // recaptures where only order/chrome changed but no new message appeared.
    88	            if !recordNovelFingerprints(input.content, threadID: threadID, nowMs: nowMs, d) {
    89	                return .deduplicated
    90	            }
    91	
    92	            // 2. Freeze-then-create: seal mutable versions from past hours.
    93	            try d.execute(sql: "UPDATE versions SET is_frozen=1 WHERE thread_id=? AND is_frozen=0 AND hour_bucket<>?",
    94	                          arguments: [threadID, bucket])
    95	
    96	            // 3. Upsert this hour's version (replace content, reset pending, un-freeze if clock stepped back).
    97	            if let vid = try String.fetchOne(d, sql: "SELECT id FROM versions WHERE thread_id=? AND hour_bucket=?",
    98	                                             arguments: [threadID, bucket]) {
    99	                try d.execute(sql: """
   100	                    UPDATE versions SET content=?, content_hash=?, word_count=?, committed_at=?,
   101	                                        extract_status='pending', is_frozen=0 WHERE id=?
   102	                    """, arguments: [storedContent, hash, words, nowMs, vid])
   103	                return .committed(versionID: vid, contentHash: hash)
   104	            } else {
   105	                let vid = Ident.uuidv7(nowMs: nowMs)
   106	                try d.execute(sql: """
   107	                    INSERT INTO versions (id, thread_id, hour_bucket, content, content_hash, word_count, is_frozen, committed_at, extract_status)
   108	                    VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,0,?,'pending')
   109	                    """, arguments: [vid, threadID, bucket, storedContent, hash, words, nowMs])
   110	                return .committed(versionID: vid, contentHash: hash)
   111	            }
   112	        }
   113	    }
   114	}
   115	
   116	extension Store {
   117	    public func pendingWork(nowMs: EpochMs, idleThresholdMs: EpochMs) throws -> [PendingVersion] {
   118	        // Note: failed-baseline edge is accepted M1 semantics (an extract_status='failed' earlier version
   119	        // can serve as baseline; its unextracted facts are suppressed from the newer diff).
   120	        try db.dbQueue.read { d in
   121	            let currentBucket = HourBucket.bucket(forMs: nowMs)
   122	            let rows = try Row.fetchAll(d, sql: """
   123	                SELECT v.id, v.thread_id, v.hour_bucket, v.content, v.content_hash,
   124	                       t.source_app, t.source_key,
   125	                       (SELECT p.content FROM versions p
   126	                         WHERE p.thread_id = v.thread_id AND p.hour_bucket < v.hour_bucket
   127	                         ORDER BY p.hour_bucket DESC LIMIT 1) AS previous_frozen_content
   128	                FROM versions v JOIN threads t ON t.id = v.thread_id
   129	                WHERE v.extract_status = 'pending'
   130	                  AND (v.is_frozen = 1 OR v.hour_bucket < ? OR v.committed_at <= ?)
   131	                  AND NOT EXISTS (
   132	                    SELECT 1 FROM retry_queue r
   133	                    WHERE r.kind = 'extract' AND r.version_id = v.id AND r.next_attempt_at > ?
   134	                  )
   135	                ORDER BY v.committed_at
   136	                """, arguments: [currentBucket, nowMs - idleThresholdMs, nowMs])
   137	            return rows.map { r in
   138	                PendingVersion(id: r["id"], threadID: r["thread_id"], hourBucket: r["hour_bucket"],
   139	                               content: decryptOrMarker(r["content"]), contentHash: r["content_hash"],
   140	                               sourceApp: r["source_app"], sourceKey: r["source_key"],
   141	                               previousFrozenContent: (r["previous_frozen_content"] as String?).map(decryptOrMarker))
   142	            }
   143	        }
   144	    }

   147	        try db.dbQueue.write { d in
   148	            try d.execute(sql: "UPDATE versions SET extract_status='completed' WHERE id=? AND content_hash=?",
   149	                          arguments: [versionID, contentHashRead])
   150	            return d.changesCount > 0
   151	        }
   152	    }
   153	
   154	    public func markExtractFailed(versionID: String) throws {
   155	        try db.dbQueue.write { d in
   156	            try d.execute(sql: "UPDATE versions SET extract_status='failed' WHERE id=?", arguments: [versionID])
   157	        }
   158	    }
   159	
   160	    public func insertDerivatives(versionID: String, threadID: String, facts: [String], nowMs: EpochMs) throws -> [PendingDerivative] {
   161	        try db.dbQueue.write { d in
   162	            var inserted: [PendingDerivative] = []
   163	            for fact in facts {
   164	                let id = Ident.uuidv7(nowMs: nowMs)
   165	                let hash = ContentHash.sha256Hex(fact)
   166	                let storedContent = try cipher.encrypt(fact)
   167	                try d.execute(sql: """
   168	                    INSERT OR IGNORE INTO derivatives (id, thread_id, version_id, content, content_hash, committed_at, embedding_status)
   169	                    VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,'pending')
   170	                    """, arguments: [id, threadID, versionID, storedContent, hash, nowMs])
   171	                if d.changesCount > 0 { inserted.append(PendingDerivative(id: id, content: fact)) }
   172	            }
   173	            return inserted
   174	        }
   175	    }

   179	            try d.execute(sql: "UPDATE derivatives SET embedding_status='completed' WHERE id=?", arguments: [derivativeID])
   180	        }

     5	extension Store {
     6	    public func pausedApps() throws -> Set<String> { try readSet("paused_apps") }
     7	    public func pausedThreads() throws -> Set<String> { try readSet("paused_threads") }
     8	
     9	    public func setAppPaused(_ bundleID: String, paused: Bool, nowMs: EpochMs) throws {
    10	        try mutateSet("paused_apps", element: bundleID, insert: paused, nowMs: nowMs)
    11	    }
    12	    public func setThreadPaused(_ sourceKey: String, paused: Bool, nowMs: EpochMs) throws {
    13	        try mutateSet("paused_threads", element: sourceKey, insert: paused, nowMs: nowMs)
    14	    }
    15	
    16	    func readSet(_ key: String) throws -> Set<String> {
    17	        try db.dbQueue.read { d in
    18	            guard let json = try String.fetchOne(d, sql: "SELECT value FROM settings WHERE key=?", arguments: [key]) else { return [] }
    19	            // Recoverable metadata: log decode failure and treat as empty.
    20	            guard let arr = try? JSONDecoder().decode([String].self, from: Data(json.utf8)) else {
    21	                NSLog("MaxMi: paused-set '\(key)' JSON decode failed, treating as empty: \(json)")
    22	                return []
    23	            }
    24	            return Set(arr)
    25	        }
    26	    }
    27	
    28	    func mutateSet(_ key: String, element: String, insert: Bool, nowMs: EpochMs) throws {
    29	        try db.dbQueue.write { d in
    30	            var set: Set<String> = []
    31	            if let json = try String.fetchOne(d, sql: "SELECT value FROM settings WHERE key=?", arguments: [key]) {
    32	                // Recoverable metadata: log decode failure and treat as empty.
    33	                if let arr = try? JSONDecoder().decode([String].self, from: Data(json.utf8)) {
    34	                    set = Set(arr)
    35	                } else {
    36	                    NSLog("MaxMi: paused-set '\(key)' JSON decode failed, treating as empty: \(json)")
    37	                }
    38	            }
    39	            if insert { set.insert(element) } else { set.remove(element) }
    40	            let json = String(decoding: try JSONEncoder().encode(set.sorted()), as: UTF8.self)
    41	            try d.execute(sql: "INSERT OR REPLACE INTO settings VALUES (?,?,?)", arguments: [key, json, nowMs])
    42	        }
    43	    }
    44	}
     1	import CryptoKit
     2	import Foundation
     3	
     4	public enum CipherError: Error, Equatable {
     5	    case integrityFailure       // authentication failed: tampered data or wrong key
     6	    case malformedCiphertext    // prefixed but not decodable as nonce+ct+tag
     7	    case keyUnavailable         // no encryption key (Keychain locked/denied); refuse to read/write
     8	}
     9	
    10	/// Encrypts/decrypts individual TEXT column values. Minimi-parity wire format:
    11	/// "enc:v1:" + base64(nonce[12] ‖ ciphertext ‖ tag[16]), AES-256-GCM, no AAD.
    12	public protocol FieldCipher: Sendable {
    13	    func encrypt(_ plaintext: String) throws -> String
    14	    func decrypt(_ stored: String) throws -> String
    15	}
    16	
    17	public struct AESGCMFieldCipher: FieldCipher {
    18	    static let prefix = "enc:v1:"
    19	    let key: SymmetricKey
    20	
    21	    public init(keyData: Data) {
    22	        precondition(keyData.count == 32, "AES-256 needs a 32-byte key")
    23	        self.key = SymmetricKey(data: keyData)
    24	    }
    25	
    26	    public func encrypt(_ plaintext: String) throws -> String {
    27	        let sealed = try AES.GCM.seal(Data(plaintext.utf8), using: key)
    28	        // .combined is nonce ‖ ciphertext ‖ tag for the default 12-byte nonce.
    29	        return Self.prefix + sealed.combined!.base64EncodedString()
    30	    }
    31	
    32	    public func decrypt(_ stored: String) throws -> String {
    33	        guard stored.hasPrefix(Self.prefix) else { return stored }   // passthrough: pre-M3 rows
    34	        guard let blob = Data(base64Encoded: String(stored.dropFirst(Self.prefix.count))),
    35	              blob.count >= 12 + 16,
    36	              let box = try? AES.GCM.SealedBox(combined: blob) else {
    37	            throw CipherError.malformedCiphertext
    38	        }
    39	        guard let plain = try? AES.GCM.open(box, using: key) else {
    40	            throw CipherError.integrityFailure
    41	        }
    42	        return String(decoding: plain, as: UTF8.self)
    43	    }
    44	}
    45	
    46	public extension AESGCMFieldCipher {
    47	    /// Deterministic key for tests. Never used outside test targets.
    48	    static var testCipher: AESGCMFieldCipher { AESGCMFieldCipher(keyData: Data(repeating: 7, count: 32)) }
    49	}
    50	
    51	/// A cipher that refuses to operate. Used as the Store's cipher when the real
    52	/// encryption key is unavailable (Keychain locked/denied): every write throws
    53	/// and rolls back rather than silently producing recoverable-by-anyone
    54	/// ciphertext under a known key. This pushes the "no plaintext-equivalent
    55	/// writes without a key" invariant into the type system instead of relying on
    56	/// a control-flow guard staying ahead of every write path (spec §9).
    57	public struct UnavailableCipher: FieldCipher {
    58	    public init() {}
    59	    public func encrypt(_ plaintext: String) throws -> String { throw CipherError.keyUnavailable }
    60	    public func decrypt(_ stored: String) throws -> String {
    61	        // Passthrough for genuinely-unprefixed values (harmless), refuse to
    62	        // pretend we can read anything that claims to be encrypted.
    63	        guard stored.hasPrefix(AESGCMFieldCipher.prefix) else { return stored }
    64	        throw CipherError.keyUnavailable
    65	    }
    66	}

diff --git a/Sources/MaxMi/SettingsWindow.swift b/Sources/MaxMi/SettingsWindow.swift
new file mode 100644
index 0000000..c995476
--- /dev/null
+++ b/Sources/MaxMi/SettingsWindow.swift
@@ -0,0 +1,39 @@
+import AppKit
+import SwiftUI
+import MaxMiUI
+
+@MainActor
+final class SettingsWindow {
+    private var window: NSWindow?
+    private let viewModel: SettingsViewModel
+
+    init(viewModel: SettingsViewModel) {
+        self.viewModel = viewModel
+    }
+
+    func show() {
+        if window == nil {
+            let window = NSWindow(
+                contentRect: NSRect(x: 0, y: 0, width: 500, height: 500),
+                styleMask: [.titled, .closable, .resizable],
+                backing: .buffered,
+                defer: false
+            )
+            window.title = "MaxMi Settings"
+            window.center()
+            window.contentViewController = NSHostingController(rootView: SettingsView(
+                viewModel: viewModel
+            ))
+            window.setFrameAutosaveName("SettingsWindow")
+            self.window = window
+        }
+
+        // Refresh the view model on show so launch-at-login status reflects external changes
+        Task {
+            await viewModel.refresh()
+        }
+
+        NSApp.activate(ignoringOtherApps: true)
+        window?.makeKeyAndOrderFront(nil)
+    }
+}
diff --git a/Sources/MaxMiStore/ActivityStore.swift b/Sources/MaxMiStore/ActivityStore.swift
index a73edca..a9d4a0a 100644
--- a/Sources/MaxMiStore/ActivityStore.swift
+++ b/Sources/MaxMiStore/ActivityStore.swift
@@ -284,6 +284,22 @@ extension Store {
         }
     }
 
+    public func observedActivityApps() throws -> [(bundle: String, label: String)] {
+        try db.dbQueue.read { d in
+            let rows = try Row.fetchAll(d, sql: """
+                SELECT app_bundle, app_label
+                FROM (
+                    SELECT app_bundle, app_label, started_at,
+                           ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY app_bundle ORDER BY started_at DESC) AS rn
+                    FROM activity_sessions
+                )
+                WHERE rn = 1
+                ORDER BY app_label
+                """)
+            return rows.map { (bundle: $0["app_bundle"], label: $0["app_label"]) }
+        }
+    }
